"><h1 id="langgraph-python-sdk">LangGraph Python SDK</h1>
<p><a href="https://pypi.org/project/langgraph-sdk/#history"><img src="https://img.shields.io/pypi/v/langgraph-sdk?label=%20" alt="PyPI - Version"></a>
<a href="https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT"><img src="https://img.shields.io/pypi/l/langgraph-sdk" alt="PyPI - License"></a>
<a href="https://pypistats.org/packages/langgraph-sdk"><img src="https://img.shields.io/pepy/dt/langgraph-sdk" alt="PyPI - Downloads"></a>
<a href="https://x.com/langchain_oss"><img src="https://img.shields.io/twitter/url/https/twitter.com/langchain_oss.svg?style=social&#x26;label=Follow%20%40LangChain" alt="Twitter"></a></p>
<p>To help you ship LangGraph apps to production faster, check out <a href="https://www.langchain.com/langsmith">LangSmith</a>.
<a href="https://www.langchain.com/langsmith">LangSmith</a> is a unified developer platform for building, testing, and monitoring LLM applications.</p>
<h2 id="quick-install">Quick Install</h2>
<pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">uv</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> add</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> langgraph-sdk</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="-what-is-this">🤔 What is this?</h2>
<p>This library provides the Python SDK for interacting with the LangGraph API. Use it to connect to a running LangGraph API server, manage assistants and threads, and stream runs from Python applications.</p>
<p>You will need a running LangGraph API server. If you're running a server locally using <code>langgraph-cli</code>, the SDK will automatically point at <code>http://localhost:8123</code>; otherwise, specify the server URL when creating a client.</p>
<h2 id="-documentation">📖 Documentation</h2>
<p>For full documentation, see the <a href="https://reference.langchain.com/python/langgraph-sdk/">API reference</a>. For conceptual guides and tutorials, see the <a href="https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/langgraph/overview">LangGraph Docs</a>.</p>
<h2 id="quick-start">Quick Start</h2>
<pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> langgraph_sdk </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> get_client</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># If you're using a remote server, initialize the client with `get_client(url=REMOTE_URL)`</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">client </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> get_client()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># List all assistants</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">assistants </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> client.assistants.search()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># We auto-create an assistant for each graph you register in config.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">agent </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> assistants[</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">0</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Start a new thread</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">thread </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> client.threads.create()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># Start a streaming run</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">input</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> {</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"messages"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [{</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"role"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"human"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"content"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"what's the weather in la"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}]}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> chunk </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> client.runs.stream(thread[</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">'thread_id'</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], agent[</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">'assistant_id'</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">], </span><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">input</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">input</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(chunk)</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="known-limitations">Known Limitations</h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>WebSocket transport</strong> requires <code>websockets>=14</code> and is only available on the async client (<code>AsyncThreadStream</code>). The sync client (<code>SyncThreadStream</code>) uses SSE exclusively.</li>
<li><strong><code>thread.extensions[name]</code></strong> opens a new subscription each time the same name is accessed. Assign the projection to a variable and reuse it within a single session rather than re-indexing across multiple iterations.</li>
<li><strong>Sync streaming</strong> drives the lifecycle watcher in a background thread. Long-lived sync sessions will hold that thread open until the context manager exits.</li>
<li><strong>Reconnect attempts</strong> are limited to 5 by default for both the shared SSE fan-out and the lifecycle watcher. Persistent network partitions will surface as <code>RuntimeError</code> on in-flight projections.</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="thread-centric-streaming-v3">Thread-Centric Streaming (v3)</h2>
<p><code>client.threads.stream()</code> returns a context manager that owns the SSE session for one thread. Typed projections — values snapshots, message streams, tool calls, custom events — all share the same underlying connection.</p>
<pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> langgraph_sdk </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> get_client</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> asyncio</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">client </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> get_client()</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> with</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> client.threads.stream(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    thread_id</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"my-thread"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">    assistant_id</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"agent"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">as</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> thread:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> thread.run.start(</span><span style="color:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">input</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"messages"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: [{</span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"role"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"user"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"content"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="color:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">"hi"</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}]})</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    # Start all consumers concurrently so they share one SSE connection.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    async</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> def</span><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> get_messages</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">():</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">        return</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [s </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> s </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> thread.messages]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    async</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> def</span><span style="color:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> get_tool_calls</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">():</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">        return</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> [c </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">async</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> c </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> thread.tool_calls]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    messages, tool_calls </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> asyncio.gather(get_messages(), get_tool_calls())</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">    for</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> stream </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">in</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> messages:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">        print</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> stream.text)          </span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># accumulated text</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">    final </span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">=</span><span style="color:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> await</span><span style="color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> thread.output           </span><span style="color:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"># terminal state values</span></span></code></pre>

langgraph_sdk\n\n\u003e Python package\n\n📖 [View in docs](https://reference.langchain.com/python/langgraph-sdk)\n\n# LangGraph Python SDK\n\n[![PyPI - Version](https://img.shields.io/pypi/v/langgraph-sdk?label=%20)](https://pypi.org/project/langgraph-sdk/#history)\n[![PyPI - License](https://img.shields.io/pypi/l/langgraph-sdk)](https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT)\n[![PyPI - Downloads](https://img.shields.io/pepy/dt/langgraph-sdk)](https://pypistats.org/packages/langgraph-sdk)\n[![Twitter](https://img.shields.io/twitter/url/https/twitter.com/langchain_oss.svg?style=social\u0026label=Follow%20%40LangChain)](https://x.com/langchain_oss)\n\nTo help you ship LangGraph apps to production faster, check out [LangSmith](https://www.langchain.com/langsmith).\n[LangSmith](https://www.langchain.com/langsmith) is a unified developer platform for building, testing, and monitoring LLM applications.\n\n## Quick Install\n\n```bash\nuv add langgraph-sdk\n```\n\n## 🤔 What is this?\n\nThis library provides the Python SDK for interacting with the LangGraph API. Use it to connect to a running LangGraph API server, manage assistants and threads, and stream runs from Python applications.\n\nYou will need a running LangGraph API server. If you're running a server locally using `langgraph-cli`, the SDK will automatically point at `http://localhost:8123`; otherwise, specify the server URL when creating a client.\n\n## 📖 Documentation\n\nFor full documentation, see the [API reference](https://reference.langchain.com/python/langgraph-sdk/). For conceptual guides and tutorials, see the [LangGraph Docs](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/langgraph/overview).\n\n## Quick Start\n\n```python\nfrom langgraph_sdk import get_client\n\n# If you're using a remote server, initialize the client with `get_client(url=REMOTE_URL)`\nclient = get_client()\n\n# List all assistants\nassistants = await client.assistants.search()\n\n# We auto-create an assistant for each graph you register in config.\nagent = assistants[0]\n\n# Start a new thread\nthread = await client.threads.create()\n\n# Start a streaming run\ninput = {\"messages\": [{\"role\": \"human\", \"content\": \"what's the weather in la\"}]}\nasync for chunk in client.runs.stream(thread['thread_id'], agent['assistant_id'], input=input):\n    print(chunk)\n```\n\n## Known Limitations\n\n- **WebSocket transport** requires `websockets\u003e=14` and is only available on the async client (`AsyncThreadStream`). The sync client (`SyncThreadStream`) uses SSE exclusively.\n- **`thread.extensions[name]`** opens a new subscription each time the same name is accessed. Assign the projection to a variable and reuse it within a single session rather than re-indexing across multiple iterations.\n- **Sync streaming** drives the lifecycle watcher in a background thread. Long-lived sync sessions will hold that thread open until the context manager exits.\n- **Reconnect attempts** are limited to 5 by default for both the shared SSE fan-out and the lifecycle watcher. Persistent network partitions will surface as `RuntimeError` on in-flight projections.\n\n## Thread-Centric Streaming (v3)\n\n`client.threads.stream()` returns a context manager that owns the SSE session for one thread. Typed projections — values snapshots, message streams, tool calls, custom events — all share the same underlying connection.\n\n```python\nfrom langgraph_sdk import get_client\nimport asyncio\n\nclient = get_client()\n\nasync with client.threads.stream(\n    thread_id=\"my-thread\",\n    assistant_id=\"agent\",\n) as thread:\n    await thread.run.start(input={\"messages\": [{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": \"hi\"}]})\n\n    # Start all consumers concurrently so they share one SSE connection.\n    async def get_messages():\n        return [s async for s in thread.messages]\n\n    async def get_tool_calls():\n        return [c async for c in thread.tool_calls]\n\n    messages, tool_calls = await asyncio.gather(get_messages(), get_tool_calls())\n\n    for stream in messages:\n        print(await stream.text)          # accumulated text\n\n    final = await thread.output           # terminal state values\n```\n\n## 📕 Releases \u0026 Versioning\n\nSee our [Releases](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/release-policy) and [Versioning](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/versioning) policies.\n\n## 💁 Contributing\n\nAs an open-source project in a rapidly developing field, we are extremely open to contributions, whether it be in the form of a new feature, improved infrastructure, or better documentation.\n\nFor detailed information on how to contribute, see the [Contributing Guide](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/contributing/overview).\n\n## Classes\n\n- this?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis library provides the Python SDK for interacting with the LangGraph API. Use it to connect to a running LangGraph API server, manage assistants and threads, and stream runs from Python applications.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou will need a running LangGraph API server. If you're running a server locally using \u003ccode\u003elanggraph-cli\u003c/code\u003e, the SDK will automatically point at \u003ccode\u003ehttp://localhost:8123\u003c/code\u003e; otherwise, specify the server URL when creating a client.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"-documentation\"\u003e📖 Documentation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFor full documentation, see the \u003ca href=\"https://reference.langchain.com/python/langgraph-sdk/\"\u003eAPI reference\u003c/a\u003e. print\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"color:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8\"\u003e(chunk)\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"known-limitations\"\u003eKnown Limitations\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWebSocket transport\u003c/strong\u003e requires \u003ccode\u003ewebsockets\u003e=14\u003c/code\u003e and is only available on the async client (\u003ccode\u003eAsyncThreadStream\u003c/code\u003e). The sync client (\u003ccode\u003eSyncThreadStream\u003c/code\u003e) uses SSE exclusively.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e\u003ccode\u003ethread.extensions[name]\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e opens a new subscription each time the same name is accessed. Assign the projection to a variable and reuse it within a single session rather than re-indexing across multiple iterations.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSync streaming\u003c/strong\u003e drives the lifecycle watcher in a background thread. Long-lived sync sessions will hold that thread open until the context manager exits.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReconnect attempts\u003c/strong\u003e are limited to 5 by default for both the shared SSE fan-out and the lifecycle watcher. Persistent network partitions will surface as \u003ccode\u003eRuntimeError\u003c/code\u003e on in-flight projections.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2 id=\"thread-centric-streaming-v3\"\u003eThread-Centric Streaming (v3)\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ccode\u003eclient.threads.stream()\u003c/code\u003e returns a context manager that owns the SSE session for one thread. Typed projections — values snapshots, message streams, tool calls, custom events — all share the same underlying connection.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre class=\"shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark\" style=\"background-color:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e;color:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8\" tabindex=\"0\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003e\u003cspan class=\"line\"\u003e\u003cspan Version](https://img.shields.io/pypi/v/langgraph-sdk?label=%20)](https://pypi.org/project/langgraph-sdk/#history)\n[![PyPI - License](https://img.shields.io/pypi/l/langgraph-sdk)](https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT)\n[![PyPI - Downloads](https://img.shields.io/pepy/dt/langgraph-sdk)](https://pypistats.org/packages/langgraph-sdk)\n[![Twitter](https://img.shields.io/twitter/url/https/twitter.com/langchain_oss.svg?style=social\u0026label=Follow%20%40LangChain)](https://x.com/langchain_oss)\n\nTo help you ship LangGraph apps to production faster, check out [LangSmith](https://www.langchain.com/langsmith).\n[LangSmith](https://www.langchain.com/langsmith) is a unified developer platform for building, testing, and monitoring LLM applications.\n\n## Quick Install\n\n```bash\nuv add langgraph-sdk\n```\n\n## 🤔 What is this?\n\nThis library provides the Python SDK for interacting with the LangGraph API. Use it to connect to a running LangGraph API server, manage assistants and threads, and stream runs from Python applications.\n\nYou will need a running LangGraph API server. If you're running a server locally using `langgraph-cli`, the SDK will automatically point at `http://localhost:8123`; otherwise, specify the server URL when creating a client.\n\n## 📖 Documentation\n\nFor full documentation, see the [API reference](https://reference.langchain.com/python/langgraph-sdk/). For conceptual guides and tutorials, see the [LangGraph Docs](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/langgraph/overview).\n\n## Quick Start\n\n```python\nfrom langgraph_sdk import get_client\n\n# If you're using a remote server, initialize the client with `get_client(url=REMOTE_URL)`\nclient = get_client()\n\n# List all assistants\nassistants = await client.assistants.search()\n\n# We auto-create an assistant for each graph you register in config.\nagent = assistants[0]\n\n# Start a new thread\nthread = await client.threads.create()\n\n# Start a streaming run\ninput = {\"messages\": [{\"role\": \"human\", \"content\": \"what's the weather in la\"}]}\nasync for chunk in client.runs.stream(thread['thread_id'], agent['assistant_id'], input=input):\n    print(chunk)\n```\n\n## Known Limitations\n\n- **WebSocket transport** requires `websockets\u003e=14` and is only available on the async client (`AsyncThreadStream`). The sync client (`SyncThreadStream`) uses SSE exclusively.\n- **`thread.extensions[name]`** opens a new subscription each time the same name is accessed. Assign the projection to a variable and reuse it within a single session rather than re-indexing across multiple iterations.\n- **Sync streaming** drives the lifecycle watcher in a background thread. Long-lived sync sessions will hold that thread open until the context manager exits.\n- **Reconnect attempts** are limited to 5 by default for both the shared SSE fan-out and the lifecycle watcher. Persistent network partitions will surface as `RuntimeError` on in-flight projections.\n\n## Thread-Centric Streaming (v3)\n\n`client.threads.stream()` returns a context manager that owns the SSE session for one thread. Typed projections — values snapshots, message streams, tool calls, custom events — all share the same underlying connection.\n\n```python\nfrom langgraph_sdk import get_client\nimport asyncio\n\nclient = get_client()\n\nasync with client.threads.stream(\n    thread_id=\"my-thread\",\n    assistant_id=\"agent\",\n) as thread:\n    await thread.run.start(input={\"messages\": [{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": \"hi\"}]})\n\n    # Start all consumers concurrently so they share one SSE connection.\n    async def get_messages():\n        return [s async for s in thread.messages]\n\n    async def get_tool_calls():\n        return [c async for c in thread.tool_calls]\n\n    messages, tool_calls = await asyncio.gather(get_messages(), get_tool_calls())\n\n    for stream in messages:\n        print(await stream.text)          # accumulated text\n\n    final = await thread.output           # terminal state values\n```\n\n## 📕 Releases \u0026 Versioning\n\nSee our [Releases](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/release-policy) and [Versioning](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/versioning) policies.\n\n## 💁 Contributing\n\nAs an open-source project in a rapidly developing field, we are extremely open to contributions, whether it be in the form of a new feature, improved infrastructure, or better documentation.\n\nFor detailed information on how to contribute, see the [Contributing Guide](https://docs.langchain.com/oss/python/contributing/overview)."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"24:[\"$\",\"$L118\",null,{\"html\":\"$119\",\"rawContent\":\"$11a\",\"className\":\"\",\"compact\":false}]\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"117:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-8xl
